3. 百分比字段用数值，不带%符号。
4. 评估必须基于其他Agent输出汇总后再给出分数与结论。

输出JSON结构：
{
  "agent": "commander",
  "summary": "string",
  "metrics": {
    "price": number,
    "changePercent": number,
    "turnoverRate": number,
    "innerVolume": number|null,
    "outerVolume": number|null,
    "sector": "string|null",
    "date": "YYYY-MM-DD"
  },
  "recommendation": {
    "entryScore": number,
    "valuationScore": number,
    "confidence": number,
    "rating": "string"
  },
  "reasons": ["string"],
  "risks": ["string"],
  "chart": null
}
